class="text-2xl @xs:text-3xl @lg:text-4xl leading-tight font-bold flex items-center gap-[.5em] grow text-pretty clear-right xs:clear-none">Web API</h1><p class="max-w-3xl w-full text-lg text-tint clear-both">SonarQube provides the Web API to access its functionalities from applications.</p></header><div class="flex flex-col [&amp;&gt;*+*]:mt-5 whitespace-pre-wrap"><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">The web services composing the <span data-state="closed"><a class="underline decoration-[max(0.07em,1px)] underline-offset-2 links-accent:underline-offset-4 links-default:decoration-primary/6 links-default:text-primary-subtle hover:links-default:text-primary-strong contrast-more:links-default:text-primary duration-100" href="https://next.sonarqube.com/sonarqube/web_api" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">web API<svg viewBox="0 0 384 512" fill="currentColor" style="overflow:visible" class="gb-icon ml-0.5 inline size-3 links-accent:text-tint-subtle"><path fill="currentColor" d="M360 64c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24l0 240c0 13.3-10.7 24-24 24s-24-10.7-24-24l0-182.1-295 295c-9.4 9.4-24.6 To access the documentation, click the help menu from the top bar and select Web API or Web API v2.</p><div class="decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl layout-wide:max-w-6xl mx-auto print:break-inside-avoid Web API as endpoints get deprecated and replaced.</p><h2 id="authenticate-to-api" class="text-xl @xs:text-2xl @lg:text-3xl font-semibold heading pdf-heading flex items-baseline justify-self-start max-w-full break-words text-start self-start justify-start leading-tight">Authenticating to the Web API</div></h2><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">Administrative web services are secured and require the user to have specific permissions.</p><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">To authenticate to the Web API, we recommend that you use the bearer authentication scheme.</p><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">If you cannot use the bearer authentication scheme (e.g., with the API endpoint <span data-state="closed"><a class="underline decoration-[max(0.07em,1px)] underline-offset-2 links-accent:underline-offset-4 links-default:decoration-primary/6 links-default:text-primary-subtle hover:links-default:text-primary-strong contrast-more:links-default:text-primary contrast-more:hover:links-default:text-primary-strong links-accent:decoration-primary-subtle hover:links-accent:decoration-[3px] hover:links-accent:[text-decoration-skip-ink:none] transition-all duration-100" href="https://next.sonarqube.com/sonarqube/web_api/api/monitoring/metrics" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">monitoring/metrics<svg viewBox="0 0 384 512" fill="currentColor" style="overflow:visible" class="gb-icon ml-0.5 inline size-3 links-accent:text-tint-subtle"><path fill="currentColor" d="M360 64c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24l0 240c0 13.3-10.7 24-24 24s-24-10.7-24-24l0-182.1-295 295c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0S-2.3 416.4 7 407l295-295-182.1 0c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24l240 0z"/></svg></a></span>), you can use the X-Sonar-Passcode authentication scheme.</p><details id="with-the-bearer-authentication-scheme" class="scroll-mt-(--content-scroll-margin) decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid group/expandable bg-tint-base border border-b-0 border-tint-subtle mt-0! mb-0 first:mt-5! first:rounded-t-lg [:not(&amp;)_+_&amp;]:mt-5! 33.9 0l200 200z"/></svg>With the bearer authentication scheme<a href="#with-the-bearer-authentication-scheme" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="absolute top-2 bottom-2 right-4 flex has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">With the bearer authentication scheme, a SonarQube Server token is used:</p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid min-h-lh [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start self-start justify-start">A token of <strong class="font-bold">User</strong> type is generated in SonarQube Server UI.
See <a class="underline decoration-[max(0.07em,1px)] underline-offset-2 links-accent:underline-offset-4 links-default:decoration-primary/6 links-default:text-primary-subtle hover:links-default:text-primary-strong contrast-more:links-default:text-primary contrast-more:hover:links-default:text-primary-strong links-accent:decoration-primary-subtle hover:links-accent:decoration-[3px] hover:links-accent:[text-decoration-skip-ink:none] transition-all duration-100" href="/sonarqube-server/user-guide/managing-tokens">Managing your tokens</a>.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid min-h-lh [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start self-start justify-start">It is provided through the <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">Authorization: Bearer &lt;myToken&gt;</code> header.
See <!-- --><strong class="font-bold">Sample API request</strong> below.<!-- --></p></div></li></ul><div class="hint transition-colors rounded-corners:rounded-md circular-corners:rounded-xl overflow-hidden bg-info border-info theme-muted-tint:bg-info-solid/2 [html.sidebar-filled.theme-bold.tint_&amp;]:bg-info-solid/2 text-sm grid grid-cols-[auto_1fr] decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid" aria-label="Information" role="note"><div class="py-4 pl-4 text-info-subtle contrast-more:text-info"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512" fill="currentColor" style="overflow:visible" class="gb-icon size-[1.2em] mt-px leading-normal"><path fill="currentColor" d="M256 48a208 208 0 1 1 0 416 208 208 0 1 1 0-416zm0 464a256 256 0 1 0 0-512 256 256 0 1 0 0 512zM216 336c-13.3 0-24 10.7-24 24s10.7 24 24 24l80 0c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24s-10.7-24-24-24l-8 0 0-88c0-13.3-10.7-24-24-24l-48 0c-13.3 0-24 10.7-24 24s10.7 24 24 24l24 0 0 64-24 0zm40-144a32 32 0 1 0 0-64 32 32 0 1 0 0 64z"/></svg></div><div class="p-4 pl-3 empty:p-0 -row-end-1 -col-end-1 space-y-3 [&amp;_.hint]:border [&amp;_pre]:border [&amp;_pre]:border-neutral"><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-neutral-strong [&amp;_.can-override-bg]:bg-neutral-active [&amp;_.can-override-text]:text-neutral-strong flip-heading-hash text-start self-start justify-start">If a token is used to interact with the API, a <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">SonarQube-Authentication-Token-Expiration</code> HTTP header is added to the response. This header contains the token expiration date and can help third-party tools track upcoming expirations; this method allows the token to be rotated in time.</p></div></div></div></details><details id="with-the-x-sonar-passcode-authentication-scheme" class="scroll-mt-(--content-scroll-margin) decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid group/expandable bg-tint-base border border-b-0 border-tint-subtle mt-0! mb-0 first:mt-5! first:rounded-t-lg [:not(&amp;)_+_&amp;]:mt-5! [:not(&amp;)_+_&amp;]:rounded-t-lg [&amp;:not(:has(+_&amp;))]:mb-5 [&amp;:not(:has(+_&amp;))]:rounded-b-lg [&amp;:not(:has(+_&amp;))]:border-b"><summary class="cursor-pointer px-4 pr-10 py-4 relative list-none select-none transition-colors text-tint group-hover/expandable:text-tint-strong group-open/expandable:text-tint-strong [&amp;::-webkit-details-marker]:hidden"><svg viewBox="0 0 320 512" [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start self-start justify-start">The passcode is provided through the <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint HTTP method and the right path for the operation that you want to use.</p><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">It’s highly recommended to use form data parameters when making POST requests to the Web API. If you use URI query parameters instead then these parameters won’t be securely passed to the endpoint.<!-- --></p><h3 id="content-type-header" class="text-lg @xs:text-xl @lg:text-2xl font-semibold z-1 justify-self-start max-w-full break-words text-start self-start justify-start leading-snug">Content-Type header</div></h3><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">Unless the Sonar Web API endpoint specifications list a specific <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">Content-Type</code> value, your request should use the following <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">Content-Type</code> header:</p><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start"><code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 application/x-www-form-urlencoded</code></p><p class="has-[.button,input]:flex has-[.button,input]:flex-wrap has-[.button,input]:gap-2 has-[.button,input]:items-center decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl w-full print:break-inside-avoid text-start self-start justify-start">This is the default <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">Content-Type</code> value set by most tools and libraries, such as <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">curl</code> and Python’s <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">requests</code> module, but you should check their documentation for proper usage.</p><h2 id="sample-api-request" class="text-xl @xs:text-2xl @lg:text-3xl font-semibold heading pdf-heading flex items-baseline scroll-mt-(--content-scroll-margin)
